### ALLEY ###
alley_night = {
	background = { #Nomads
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						AND = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/mpo_campfire_steppe.dds"
		environment = "environment_mpo_campfire_steppe"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/CE2/Events/Event_Images/mpo_campfire_steppe"
	}
	background = { #East Asia
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char.location ?= {
					OR = {
						culture ?= { has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						culture ?= { has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_alley_night_asia.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_alley_night_asia"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_alley_night_asia"
	}
	background = { #LotR Wood Elf
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location = {
						graphical_wilderness_all_forests_trigger = yes
						culture = { is_elf_culture = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location = {
					graphical_wilderness_all_forests_trigger = yes
					culture = { is_elf_culture = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/lorien_night.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_alley"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/city_alley_night"
	}
	
	background = {
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/alley.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_alley"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/city_alley_night"
	}
}

alley_day = {
	background = { #Nomads
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						AND = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/mpo_camp_steppe.dds"
		environment = "environment_mpo_camp_steppe"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/CE2/Events/Event_Images/mpo_camp_steppe"
	}
	background = { #LotR Wood Elf
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location = {
						graphical_wilderness_all_forests_trigger = yes
						culture = { is_elf_culture = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location = {
					graphical_wilderness_all_forests_trigger = yes
					culture = { is_elf_culture = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/lorien_day.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_forest"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/deciduous_forest_day"
	}
	
	background = { #Eastern
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location ?= {
						OR = {
							geographical_region = graphical_mena
							geographical_region = graphical_india
							culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iranian_building_gfx }
							culture ?= { has_building_gfx = indian_building_gfx }
							culture ?= { has_building_gfx = mena_building_gfx }
	#						AND = {
	# 				 			geographical_region = world_europe_west_iberia
	# 				 			faith ?= { religion = religion:islam_religion }
	# 				 		}
						#Steppe mena fallback
					 		steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes
					 		steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						geographical_region = graphical_mena
						geographical_region = graphical_india
						culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iranian_building_gfx }
						culture ?= { has_building_gfx = indian_building_gfx }
						culture ?= { has_building_gfx = mena_building_gfx }
	#					AND = {
	# 			 			geographical_region = world_europe_west_iberia
	# 			 			faith ?= { religion = religion:islam_religion }
	# 			 		}
					#Steppe mena fallback
					 	steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes
					 	steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/market_east.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_market_east"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/town_market_middleeastern_day"
	}
	background = { #East Asia
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char.location ?= {
					OR = {
						culture = { has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						culture = { has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_alley_day_asia.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_alley_day_asia"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_alley_day_asia"
	}
	background = {
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/alley_day.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_alley_day"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/city_alley_day_western"
	}
}

### ARMORY ###
armory = {
	background = { #Nomads
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						AND = {
							is_landless_adventurer = yes
							culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					AND = {
						is_landless_adventurer = yes
						culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/mpo_tent_interior_mongol.dds"
		environment = "mpo_tent_interior_mongol" 
		ambience = "event:/DLC/CE2/Events/Event_Images/mpo_tent_interior_mongol"
	}
	background = { #LAAMPs
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = { has_government = landless_adventurer_government }
			}
			trigger_else = { has_government = landless_adventurer_government }
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep3_military_tent.dds"
		environment = "environment_ep3_military_tent_interior"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP3/SFX/Events/Event_Images/ep3_evn_eventimage_living_tent_interior"
	}
	background = {
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/armory.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_armory"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/armory"
	}
}

### BATTLEFIELD ###
battlefield = {
	background = { #Dunedain
		trigger = {
			is_commanding_army = yes
			location ?= {
				exists = province_owner # Settled
				OR  = {
					geographical_region = middleearth_west_gondor
					geographical_region = middleearth_west_arnor
					culture ?= { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_dunedain }
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/battlefield_dunedain.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_farms"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/battlefield_gloomy"
	}
	
	background = {
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/battlefield.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_battlefield"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/battlefield_gloomy"
	}
}

### CORRIDOR ###
corridor_night = {
	background = { #Nomads
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						AND = {
							is_landless_adventurer = yes
							culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					AND = {
						is_landless_adventurer = yes
						culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/mpo_campfire_steppe.dds"
		environment = "environment_mpo_campfire_steppe"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/CE2/Events/Event_Images/mpo_campfire_steppe"
	}
	background = { #LAAMPs
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = { has_government = landless_adventurer_government }
			}
			trigger_else = { has_government = landless_adventurer_government }
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep3_adventurer_background.dds"
		environment = "environment_ep3_army_camp"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP3/SFX/Events/Event_Images/ep3_evn_eventimage_campfire"
	}
	background = {	#FP3
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location ?= {
						OR = {
							culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iranian_building_gfx }
							steppe_building_gfx_use_iranian_trigger = yes
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iranian_building_gfx }
						steppe_building_gfx_use_iranian_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/fp3_courtyard_night.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_fp3_courtyard_night" 
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/castle_corridor_night"
	}
	background = {	#FP2
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						#location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iberian_building_gfx }
						#location ?= { geographical_region = world_europe_west_iberia }
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = mena_building_gfx }
						location ?= {
							steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes
						}
						location.culture ?= { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_northern_adunaic }
						location.culture ?= { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_bellakari }
						location.culture ?= { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_southern_adunaic }
					}
					NOT = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					#location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iberian_building_gfx }
					#location ?= { geographical_region = world_europe_west_iberia }
					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = mena_building_gfx }
					location ?= {
						steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes
					}
					location.culture ?= { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_northern_adunaic }
					location.culture ?= { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_bellakari }
					location.culture ?= { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_southern_adunaic }
				}
				NOT = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/fp2_corridor_night.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_fp2_corridor_night" 
		ambience = "event:/DLC/FP2/SFX/Events/corridor_night" 
	}
	background = {	#Indian Corridor
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }
					}
					NOT = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					location.culture ?= { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }
				}
				NOT = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp1_corridor_indian_night.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_bp1_corridor_indian_night"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/castle_corridor_night"
	}
	background = {	#FP1
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						# location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = norse_building_gfx }
						location ?= { fp1_should_use_norse_graphics_trigger = yes } #LotR
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						AND = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					# location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = norse_building_gfx }
					location ?= { fp1_should_use_norse_graphics_trigger = yes } #LotR
					government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal

### COURTYARD ###
courtyard = {
	background = { #Nomadic MENA
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							location.culture ?= {
								OR = {
									has_cultural_tradition = tradition_saharan_nomads
									has_cultural_tradition = tradition_desert_nomads
								}
							}
						}
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					}
					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = mena_building_gfx }
					location ?= {
						OR = {
							terrain = drylands
							terrain = desert
							terrain = oasis
							terrain = desert_mountains
							terrain = floodplains
							terrain = hills
							terrain = steppe
							terrain = red_desert
							terrain = dune_sea
							terrain = volcanic_plains
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						location.culture ?= {
							OR = {
								has_cultural_tradition = tradition_saharan_nomads
								has_cultural_tradition = tradition_desert_nomads
							}
						}
					}
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
				}
				location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = mena_building_gfx }
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						terrain = drylands
						terrain = desert
						terrain = oasis
						terrain = desert_mountains
						terrain = floodplains
						terrain = hills
						terrain = steppe
						terrain = red_desert
						terrain = dune_sea
						terrain = volcanic_plains
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/desert_nomad.dds"
		environment = "environment_travel_desert"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/desert_day"
	}
	background = { #Nomads and steppe tribals
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						AND = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							is_landless_adventurer = yes
							culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						is_landless_adventurer = yes
						culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/mpo_camp_steppe.dds"
		environment = "environment_mpo_camp_steppe"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/CE2/Events/Event_Images/mpo_camp_steppe"
	}
	background = { #Western/Northern tribals
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
					OR = {
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = western_building_gfx }
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = mediterranean_building_gfx }
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = byzantine_building_gfx }
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = norse_building_gfx }
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iberian_building_gfx }
						#LotR

courtyard_location = {
	background = { #Nomadic MENA
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							location.county ?= {
								title_province = {
									has_holding_type = tribal_holding
								}
							}
							location.culture ?= {
								OR = {
									has_cultural_tradition = tradition_saharan_nomads
									has_cultural_tradition = tradition_desert_nomads
								}
							}
						}
						location.county ?= {
							title_province = {
								OR = {
									has_holding_type = herder_holding
									has_holding_type = nomad_holding
								}
							}
						}
					}
					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = mena_building_gfx }
					location ?= {
						OR = {
							terrain = drylands
							terrain = desert
							terrain = oasis
							terrain = desert_mountains
							terrain = floodplains
							terrain = hills
							terrain = steppe
							terrain = red_desert
							terrain = dune_sea
							terrain = volcanic_plains
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						location.county ?= {
							title_province = {
								has_holding_type = tribal_holding
							}
						}
						location.culture ?= {
							OR = {
								has_cultural_tradition = tradition_saharan_nomads
								has_cultural_tradition = tradition_desert_nomads
							}
						}
					}
					location.county ?= {
						title_province = {
							OR = {
								has_holding_type = herder_holding
								has_holding_type = nomad_holding
							}
						}
					}
				}
				location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = mena_building_gfx }
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						terrain = drylands
						terrain = desert
						terrain = oasis
						terrain = desert_mountains
						terrain = floodplains
						terrain = hills
						terrain = steppe
						terrain = red_desert
						terrain = dune_sea
						terrain = volcanic_plains
					}
				}
			}
		}

### DUNGEON ###
dungeon = {
	background = {	#Nomads
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = { government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic }
			}
			trigger_else = { government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic }
			
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/fp1_tribal_prison.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_fp1_tribal_prison"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/FP1/SFX/Events/event_prison"
	}

	# Winter Locations
	background = { #forest snowy
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }

					location ?= {
						OR = {
							has_province_modifier = winter_normal_modifier
							has_province_modifier = winter_harsh_modifier
							root = { has_zud_season_in_county_trigger = { COUNTY = root.location.county } }
						}
						OR = {
							graphical_wilderness_forest_trigger = yes
							graphical_wilderness_forest_pine_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = winter_normal_modifier
						has_province_modifier = winter_harsh_modifier
						root = { has_zud_season_in_county_trigger = { COUNTY = root.location.county } }
					}
					OR = {
						graphical_wilderness_forest_trigger = yes
						graphical_wilderness_forest_pine_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}

			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }

					location = {
						graphical_wilderness_desert_rhun_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location = {

				}
			}
		}

	}

	background = { # Riverside
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				has_winter_trigger = no
				is_riverside_province = yes
				OR = {
					terrain = plains
					terrain = mountains
					terrain = hills
					terrain = steppe
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp3_riverside.dds"

	}

					location ?= {

			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location ?= {
						graphical_wilderness_steppe_trigger = yes
						OR = {
							has_holding = yes
							is_county_capital = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location ?= {
					graphical_wilderness_steppe_trigger = yes
					OR = {
						has_holding = yes
						is_county_capital = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_travel_steppe.dds"
		environment = "environment_travel_mountain_settlement"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/mountains_day"
	}

terrain_scope = {
	background = { # Riverside
		trigger = {
			scope:background_terrain_scope = {
				has_winter_trigger = no
				is_riverside_province = yes
				OR = {
					terrain = plains
					terrain = mountains
					terrain = hills
					terrain = steppe
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp3_riverside.dds"
		environment = "environment_bp3_riverside"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Grand_Activities/Hunts/ep2_event_grand_hunt_waterbank"
	}

	background = { #Rice Fields - If we have Paddy fields AND/or terraced hills
	#This goes before other terrain since it can override in many different terrains if built
		trigger = {
			scope:background_terrain_scope = {
				OR = {
					terrain = terraced_hills
					has_building_or_higher = paddy_fields_01
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_rice_fields.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_rice_fields"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_rice_fields"
	}

	background = { #Farmlands/Plains, Winter
		trigger = {
			scope:background_terrain_scope = {
				has_winter_trigger = yes

				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp3_plains_winter.dds"

terrain_activity = {
	background = { # Riverside
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:activity.activity_location
			scope:activity.activity_location ?= {
				is_riverside_province = yes
				has_winter_trigger = no
				OR = {
					terrain = plains
					terrain = mountains
					terrain = hills
					terrain = steppe
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp3_riverside.dds"
		environment = "environment_bp3_riverside"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Grand_Activities/Hunts/ep2_event_grand_hunt_waterbank"
	}

	background = { #Rice Fields - If we have Paddy fields AND/or terraced hills
	#This goes before other terrain since it can override in many different terrains if built
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:activity.activity_location
			scope:activity.activity_location ?= {
				OR = {
						terrain = terraced_hills
						has_building_or_higher = paddy_fields_01
					}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_rice_fields.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_rice_fields"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_rice_fields"
	}

	background = { # Farmlands/Plains Winter
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:activity.activity_location
			scope:activity.activity_location ?= {
				has_winter_trigger = yes

					terrain = farmlands 
					graphical_plains_trigger = yes
				}

# An expanded version for travel, more focus on locality than specific terrains
terrain_travel = {
	background = { # Bridge
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				is_riverside_province = yes
				#geographical_region = world_europe #LotR
				OR = {
					terrain = farmlands
					terrain = plains
					terrain = mountains
					terrain = hills
				}
				exists = province_owner
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_travel_bridge.dds"
		environment = "environment_travel_bridge"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/mountains_day"
	}
	
	background = { # Hobbit Farmland, settled
		trigger = {
			location = {
				OR = {
					terrain = farmlands
					terrain = hills
					terrain = plains
				}
				exists = province_owner
				culture ?= { is_hobbit_culture = yes }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/hills_hobbit.dds"
		environment = "environment_travel_farmlands"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/fields_farms_day"
	}
	background = { # Elven Farmland, settled
		trigger = {
			location = {
				OR = {
					terrain = farmlands
					terrain = hills
				}
				exists = province_owner
				culture ?= { is_elf_culture = yes }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/elven_holding.dds"
		environment = "environment_travel_farmlands"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/fields_farms_day"
	}

	background = { # Riverside
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				has_winter_trigger = no
				is_riverside_province = yes
				OR = {
					terrain = plains
					terrain = mountains
					terrain = hills
					terrain = steppe
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp3_riverside.dds"
		environment = "environment_bp3_riverside"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Grand_Activities/Hunts/ep2_event_grand_hunt_waterbank"
	}
	

	background = { #Rice Fields - If we have Paddy fields AND/or terraced hills
	#This goes before other terrain since it can override in many different terrains if built
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				OR = {
					terrain = terraced_hills
					has_building_or_higher = paddy_fields_01
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_rice_fields.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_rice_fields"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_rice_fields"
	}
	background = { # Farmland/Plains, winter
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				OR = {
					terrain = farmlands
					terrain = plains
				}
				has_winter_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp3_plains_winter.dds"
		environment = "environment_bp3_plains_winter" 
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Grand_Activities/Hunts/ep2_event_grand_hunt_praire"
	}

	background = { #Farmlands - East Asia
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				terrain = farmlands
				exists = province_owner
				culture = { has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_farm_asia.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_farm_asia"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_farm_asia"
	}

	background = { # Farmland, settled
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				terrain = farmlands
				exists = province_owner
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_travel_farm.dds"
		environment = "environment_travel_farmlands"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/fields_farms_day"
	}
	background = { # Farmland, unsettled
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				terrain = farmlands
				NOT = { exists = province_owner }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/farms.dds"
		environment = "environment_travel_farmlands"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/fields_farms_day"
	}
	background = { #plains, settled
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				graphical_plains_trigger = yes
				exists = province_owner
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_travel_hills.dds"
		environment = "environment_travel_hills_settlement"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/fields_farms_day"
	}
	background = { #plains, unsettled
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				graphical_plains_trigger = yes
				NOT = { exists = province_owner }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp1_plains.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_bp1_plains"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Grand_Activities/Hunts/ep2_event_grand_hunt_praire"
	}
	
	background = { #LotR Rhûn desert
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				graphical_wilderness_desert_rhun_trigger = yes
				exists = province_owner
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/rhun.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_desert"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/desert_day"
	}
	background = { #Desert, settled, Tribal Nomads
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				graphical_wilderness_desert_trigger = yes
				province_owner ?= { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/desert_nomad.dds"
		environment = "environment_travel_desert"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/desert_day"
	}
	background = { #Desert, settled, not Tribal
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				graphical_wilderness_desert_trigger = yes
				exists = province_owner
				NOT = { province_owner = { government_has_flag = government_is_tribal } }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/desert_settlement.dds"
		environment = "environment_travel_desert"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/desert_day"
	}
	background = { #Oasis, unsettled
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				terrain = oasis
				NOT = { exists = province_owner }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/fp4_legendary_oasis.dds"
		environment = "environment_ce1_legendary_oasis"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/FP4/fp4_magic_spring"
	}
	background = { #Desert, unsettled
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				graphical_wilderness_desert_trigger = yes
				NOT = { exists = province_owner }
			}
		}

### DOCKS ###
docks = {
	background = { #LotR Dúnedain
		trigger = { 
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location.culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_dunedain }
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location.culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_dunedain }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/docks_dunedain.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_docks"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/docks_day"
	}

	background = { #LotR Adunai
		trigger = { 
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location = { lotr_has_numenorean_culture_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location = { lotr_has_numenorean_culture_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/docks_adunai.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_docks"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/docks_day"
	}
	
	background = { #LotR Elven
		trigger = { 
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location = { is_elf = yes }
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location = { is_elf = yes }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/docks_elf.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_corridor"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/docks_day"
	}
	
	background = { #South-East Asian - Seaside Village
		trigger = {
			location = {
				is_coastal = yes
				OR = {
					steppe_building_gfx_use_southeast_asian_trigger = yes
					culture ?= {
						has_building_gfx = southeast_asian_building_gfx
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_village_sea.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_village_sea"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_docks_asia"
	}
	background = {
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						location ?= { fp3_should_use_iranian_graphics_trigger = yes }
						location ?= { geographical_region = graphical_mena }
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						AND = {
							NOR = {
								government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
								government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
							}
							location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							NOR = {
								government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
								government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
							}
							location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					location ?= { fp3_should_use_iranian_graphics_trigger = yes }
					location ?= { geographical_region = graphical_mena }
					location.culture ?= { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					AND = {
						NOR = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						}
						location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						NOR = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						}
						location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/fp3_docks.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_fp3_docks"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/docks_day"
	}
	background = {
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						# location ?= { fp1_should_use_norse_graphics_trigger = yes }
						location ?= { fp1_should_use_norse_graphics_trigger = yes } #LotR
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					# location ?= { fp1_should_use_norse_graphics_trigger = yes }

					government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp1_docks_tribal.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_bp1_docks_tribal"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/docks_day"

### FEAST ###
feast = {
		background = {	# LOTR Lasgalen
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { exists = scope:activity }
				}
				location.culture ?= { is_elf_culture = yes }
				location.county ?= title:c_aradhrynd
			}
			trigger_else = {
				scope:activity.activity_location.culture ?= { is_elf_culture = yes }
				scope:activity.activity_location.county ?= title:c_aradhrynd
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/throneroom_thranduils_halls.dds"
		environment = "environment_frontend_east_main"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/feasthall"
	}
	background = {	# LOTR Elven Mallorn Forest
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { exists = scope:activity }
				}
				location.culture ?= { is_elf_culture = yes }
				location ?= { terrain = mallorn_forest }
			}
			trigger_else = {
				scope:activity.activity_location.culture ?= { is_elf_culture = yes }
				scope:activity.activity_location ?= { terrain = mallorn_forest }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/lorien_night.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_alley"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/feasthall"
	}
	background = {	# LOTR Elven+Druedain Forest
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { exists = scope:activity }
				}
				location.culture ?= {
					OR = {
						is_elf_culture = yes
						is_druedain_culture = yes
					}
				}
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						terrain = forest
						terrain = deep_forest
						terrain = jungle
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				scope:activity.activity_location.culture ?= {
					OR = {
						is_elf_culture = yes
						is_druedain_culture = yes
					}
				}
				scope:activity.activity_location ?= {
					OR = {
						terrain = forest
						terrain = deep_forest
						terrain = jungle
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/fangorn.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_forest"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/feasthall"
	}
	background = {	# LOTR Dwarven
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { exists = scope:activity }
				}
				location.culture ?= { is_dwarf_culture = yes }
			}
			trigger_else = {
				scope:activity.activity_location.culture ?= { is_dwarf_culture = yes }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/kitchen_dwarven.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_bp1_kitchen_western" 
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/feasthall"
	}
	background = {	# LOTR Hobbit
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { exists = scope:activity }
				}
				location.culture ?= { is_hobbit_culture = yes }
			}
			trigger_else = {
				scope:activity.activity_location.culture ?= { is_hobbit_culture = yes }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/kitchen_hobbit.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_bp1_kitchen_western" 
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/feasthall"
	}
	background = {	# LOTR Orc Caves
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { exists = scope:activity }
				}
				location.culture ?= { is_orc_culture = yes }
				location.county ?= { is_underground_county = yes }
			}
			trigger_else = {
				scope:activity.activity_location.culture ?= { is_orc_culture = yes }

	background = { #Nomads
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						AND = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = steppe_building_gfx }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = steppe_building_gfx }
					}
				}
			}
		}

							culture ?= { has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes }
							steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						culture ?= { has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_garden_asia.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_garden_asia"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_garden_asia"
	}

		environment = "environment_event_garden"

						culture ?= { is_elf_culture = yes }

				location = {

				 		steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes

			}

						}

sitting_room = {
	background = {	#Hobbit
		trigger = {	
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location.culture ?= { is_hobbit_culture = yes }
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { location.culture ?= { is_hobbit_culture = yes } }
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/relaxing_room_hobbit.dds"

	background = { #Nomads
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						AND = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							is_landless_adventurer = yes
							culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal

					}
					AND = {
						is_landless_adventurer = yes
						culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
				}

		}

		ambience = "event:/DLC/FP2/SFX/Events/relaxing_room"
	}
	background = { #Indians use their Study
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					location.culture ?= { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp2_study_indian.dds"
		environment = "environment_bp2_study_indian"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/office_workplace"
	}
	background = { #Japan Study
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = japanese_building_gfx }
						location ?= {
							steppe_building_gfx_use_japanese_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = japanese_building_gfx }
					location ?= {
						steppe_building_gfx_use_japanese_trigger = yes
					}
				}

		}

	}
	background = { #East Asia Study

							steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
						}
					}

							steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
						}

		environment = "environment_tgp_study_asia"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_study_asia"
	}
	background = {	#Tribal Study
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						# location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = norse_building_gfx }

### BEDCHAMBER ###
bedchamber = {
	background = { #Nomads
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						AND = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
			}
						AND = {
							is_landless_adventurer = yes
							culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						is_landless_adventurer = yes
						culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/mpo_tent_interior_mongol.dds"
		environment = "environment_mpo_tent_interior_mongol"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/CE2/Events/Event_Images/mpo_tent_interior_mongol"
	}
	background = { #LAAMPs
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					has_government = landless_adventurer_government
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				has_government = landless_adventurer_government
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep3_relaxing_tent.dds"
		environment = "environment_ep3_living_tent_interior"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP3/SFX/Events/Event_Images/ep3_evn_eventimage_living_tent_interior"
	}
	background = { #MENA
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iberian_building_gfx }
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = mena_building_gfx }
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = berber_group_building_gfx }
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = african_building_gfx }
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iranian_building_gfx }
						location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iberian_building_gfx }
					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = mena_building_gfx }
					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = berber_group_building_gfx }
					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = african_building_gfx }
					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iranian_building_gfx }
					location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_wedding_bedroom_mena.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_mena_bedchamber"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/evn_background_bedroom"
	}
	background = { #india
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					location.culture ?= { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_wedding_bedroom_indian.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_indian_bedchamber"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/evn_background_bedroom"
	}
	background = { #East Asia
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char.location ?= {
					OR = {
						culture ?= {
							has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes
						}
						steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						culture ?= {
							has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes
						}
						steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}	
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_wedding_bedroom_asia.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_wedding_bedroom_asia"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_wedding_bedroom_asia"
	}
	background = {	#Tribal Study
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						# location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = norse_building_gfx }
						location ?= { fp1_should_use_norse_graphics_trigger = yes } #LotR
						should_use_tribal_realm_palace_graphics_trigger = yes
						AND = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					# location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = norse_building_gfx }
					location ?= { fp1_should_use_norse_graphics_trigger = yes } #LotR
					should_use_tribal_realm_palace_graphics_trigger = yes
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/fp1_steward_study.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_fp1_steward_study"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/office_workplace"
	}
	
	background = {
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bedchamber.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_bedchamber"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/evn_background_bedroom"
	}

### STUDY ###
# Referenced in code, do not change the name
study = {
	background = {	#Hobbit
		trigger = {	
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location.culture ?= { is_hobbit_culture = yes }
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { location.culture ?= { is_hobbit_culture = yes } }
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/relaxing_room_hobbit.dds"
		environment = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/office_workplace"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/FP2/SFX/Events/relaxing_room"
	}
	background = { #Nomads
        trigger = {
            trigger_if = {
                limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
                scope:bg_override_char = { 
                    OR = {
                        government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
                        AND = {
                            government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
                            location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
                        }
                        AND = {
                            is_landless_adventurer = yes
                            culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            trigger_else = {
                OR = {
                    government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
                    AND = {
                        government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
                        location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
                    }
                    AND = {
                        is_landless_adventurer = yes
                        culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/mpo_tent_interior_mongol.dds"
        environment = "environment_mpo_tent_interior_mongol"
        ambience = "event:/DLC/CE2/Events/Event_Images/mpo_tent_interior_mongol"
    }
	background = { #LAAMPs
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = { has_government = landless_adventurer_government }
			}
			trigger_else = { has_government = landless_adventurer_government }
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep3_relaxing_tent.dds"
		environment = "environment_ep3_living_tent_interior"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP3/SFX/Events/Event_Images/ep3_evn_eventimage_living_tent_interior"
	}
	background = {	#Tribal Study
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						# location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = norse_building_gfx }
						location ?= { fp1_should_use_norse_graphics_trigger = yes } #LotR
						should_use_tribal_realm_palace_graphics_trigger = yes
						AND = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					# location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = norse_building_gfx }
					location ?= { fp1_should_use_norse_graphics_trigger = yes } #LotR
					should_use_tribal_realm_palace_graphics_trigger = yes
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/fp1_steward_study.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_fp1_steward_study"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/office_workplace"
	}
	background = { # Byzantium/Greek Everyone else
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						location.culture ?= {
							OR = {
								# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_byzantine
								# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_caucasian
								# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_latin
								# has_graphical_mediterranean_culture_group_trigger = yes 
								has_cultural_pillar = heritage_northern_adunaic
								has_cultural_pillar = heritage_bellakari
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					location.culture ?= {
						OR = {
							# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_byzantine
							# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_caucasian
							# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_latin

		}

		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/office_workplace"
	}
	background = { #MENA uses relaxing room as fallback
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_mena_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iranian_building_gfx }
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_african_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes }
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = berber_group_building_gfx }
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					location.culture ?= { has_graphical_mena_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iranian_building_gfx }
					location.culture ?= { has_graphical_african_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					location ?= { exists = culture steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes }
					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = berber_group_building_gfx }
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp1_relaxing_room_mena.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_bp1_relaxing_room_mena"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/office_workplace"
	}
	background = {	#Indian Study

			}

		environment = "environment_bp2_study_indian"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/office_workplace"
	}
	background = { #Japan Study
		trigger = {

					OR = {
						location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = japanese_building_gfx }

					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {

					location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = japanese_building_gfx }
					location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_japanese_trigger = yes }

		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_study_japan.dds"

#When a LAAMP is visiting someone else's study
location_study = {
	background = {	#Hobbit
		trigger = { location.culture ?= { is_hobbit_culture = yes } }
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/relaxing_room_hobbit.dds"
		environment = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/office_workplace"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/FP2/SFX/Events/relaxing_room"
	}
	background = { #Nomads
		trigger = {
			location.county.title_province ?= {
				OR = {
					has_holding_type = tribal_holding
					has_holding_type = nomad_holding
					has_holding_type = herder_holding
				}
			}
			location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/mpo_tent_interior_mongol.dds"
		environment = "environment_mpo_tent_interior_mongol"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/CE2/Events/Event_Images/mpo_tent_interior_mongol"
	}
	background = {	#Tribal Study
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				# location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = norse_building_gfx }
				location ?= { fp1_should_use_norse_graphics_trigger = yes } #LotR
				AND = {
					location.county.title_province ?= {
						OR = {
							has_holding_type = tribal_holding
							has_holding_type = nomad_holding
							has_holding_type = herder_holding
						}
					}
					location.culture ?= {
						has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = no
						has_graphical_mena_culture_group_trigger = no
						has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = no
						has_graphical_african_culture_group_trigger = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/fp1_steward_study.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_fp1_steward_study"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/office_workplace"
	}
	background = { # Byzantium/Greek Everyone else
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				location.culture ?= {
					OR = {
						# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_byzantine
						# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_caucasian
						# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_latin
						# has_graphical_mediterranean_culture_group_trigger = yes 
						has_cultural_pillar = heritage_northern_adunaic
						has_cultural_pillar = heritage_bellakari
						has_cultural_pillar = heritage_southern_adunaic
					}
				}
				location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_mediterranean_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep3_medi_study.dds"
		environment = "environment_ep3_relaxing_room"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP3/SFX/Events/Event_Images/ep3_evn_eventimage_byzantine_relaxing_room"
	}
	background = { #MENA uses relaxing room as fallback
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				location.culture ?= { has_graphical_mena_culture_group_trigger = yes }
				location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iranian_building_gfx }
				location.culture ?= { has_graphical_african_culture_group_trigger = yes }
				location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes }
				location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = berber_group_building_gfx }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp1_relaxing_room_mena.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_bp1_relaxing_room_mena"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/office_workplace"
	}
	background = {	#Indian Study
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				location.culture ?= { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
				location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }

		}

		environment = "environment_bp2_study_indian"

### RELAXING ROOM ###
relaxing_room = {
	background = {	#Hobbit
		trigger = {	
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location.culture ?= { is_hobbit_culture = yes }
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { location.culture ?= { is_hobbit_culture = yes } }
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/relaxing_room_hobbit.dds"
		environment = "environment_bp2_study_indian"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/FP2/SFX/Events/relaxing_room"
	}
	background = { #Nomads
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						AND = {
							government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
							location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
			}
						AND = {
							is_landless_adventurer = yes
							culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						is_landless_adventurer = yes
						culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/mpo_tent_interior_mongol.dds"
		environment = "environment_mpo_tent_interior_mongol"

	background = { #LAAMPs

	background = { # Byzantium/Greek Kings/Emperors
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {

						location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_mediterranean_trigger = yes }
						location.culture ?= {
							OR = {
								# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_byzantine
								# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_caucasian
								# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_latin
								# has_graphical_mediterranean_culture_group_trigger = yes 
								has_cultural_pillar = heritage_northern_adunaic
								has_cultural_pillar = heritage_bellakari
								has_cultural_pillar = heritage_southern_adunaic
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom
				OR = {
					location ?= { exists = culture steppe_building_gfx_use_mediterranean_trigger = yes }
					location.culture ?= {
						OR = {
							# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_byzantine
							# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_caucasian
							# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_latin
							# has_graphical_mediterranean_culture_group_trigger = yes

					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep3_relaxing_room.dds"
		environment = "environment_ep3_relaxing_room"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP3/SFX/Events/Event_Images/ep3_evn_eventimage_byzantine_relaxing_room"
	}

### ESTATE ###
estate = {
	background = { # Japan Estate (Domicile)
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char.domicile }
				scope:bg_override_char.domicile ?= { is_domicile_type = japanese_manor }
			}
			trigger_else = {
				domicile ?= { is_domicile_type = japanese_manor }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_moon_festival_japan.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_tanabata_festival_night_japan"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_festival_generic_japan"
	}
	background = { # Steppe Admin Estate (Domicile)
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char.domicile }
				scope:bg_override_char.domicile ?= { is_domicile_type = east_asian_estate }
				scope:bg_override_char = { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
			}
			trigger_else = {
				domicile ?= { is_domicile_type = east_asian_estate }
				has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes
			}
		}

### ARMY CAMP ###
army_camp = {
	background = { #Orcs
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = { lotr_orc_buildings = yes }
			}
			trigger_else = { lotr_orc_buildings = yes }
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/orc_camp.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_battlefield"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/camp_generic_day"
	}
	background = { #Nomads
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
						AND = {
							is_landless_adventurer = yes
							culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
					government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
					AND = {
						is_landless_adventurer = yes
						culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/mpo_hunt_steppe.dds"
		environment = "environment_mpo_hunt_steppe"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/CE2/Events/Event_Images/mpo_hunt_steppe"
	}
	background = { #East Asia
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
						culture = { has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						location = {
							steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_government = landless_adventurer_government
						location = { geographical_region = world_asia }
					}
					culture = { has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					location = {
						steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_camp_asia.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_camp_asia"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/CE2/Events/Event_Images/mpo_camp_steppe"
	}
	background = {
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/genericcamp.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_genericcamp"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/camp_generic_day"
	}
}

						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic

						}

						}
					}
				}

				}
				OR = {
				government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic

	background = {	#Norse

	}
	background = {	#MENA
		trigger = {
			scope:activity ?= {

					OR = {

					OR = {
						has_holding_type = tribal_holding
						has_holding_type = herder_holding

					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_tournament_tribal.dds"

	background = { #MENA

tournament_contest = {
	background = {
		trigger = {
			scope:activity ?= {
				activity_host = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_feudal
						government_has_flag = government_is_clan
					}
				}
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { exists = scope:contest_complete }
					OR = {
						scope:contest_complete = flag:joust
						scope:contest_complete = flag:horse_race
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					OR = {
						has_current_phase = tournament_phase_joust
						has_current_phase = tournament_phase_horse_race
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/activity_backgrounds/contest_bg_horseracing.dds"
		environment = "environment_ep2_horse_racing" 
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/camp_generic_day" 
	}
	background = {
		trigger = {
			scope:activity ?= {
				activity_host = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_feudal
						government_has_flag = government_is_clan
					}
				}
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { exists = scope:contest_complete }
					OR = {
						scope:contest_complete = flag:melee
						scope:contest_complete = flag:duel
						scope:contest_complete = flag:wrestling
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					OR = {
						has_current_phase = tournament_phase_melee
						has_current_phase = tournament_phase_duel
						has_current_phase = tournament_phase_wrestling
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/activity_backgrounds/contest_bg_melee.dds"
		environment = "environment_ep2_melee" 
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/camp_generic_day" 
	}
	background = {
		trigger = {
			scope:activity ?= {
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { exists = scope:contest_complete }
					scope:contest_complete = flag:archery
				}
				trigger_else = { has_current_phase = tournament_phase_archery }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/activity_backgrounds/contest_bg_archery.dds"
		environment = "environment_ep2_archery" 
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/camp_generic_day" 
	}
	background = {
		trigger = {
			scope:activity ?= {

		}

		environment = "environment_ep2_boardgames" 
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/corner_of_tavern" 
	}
	background = { #Tribal
		trigger = {
			scope:activity = {
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { exists = scope:contest_complete }
					scope:contest_complete = flag:recital
				}
				trigger_else = {
					OR = {
						has_current_phase = tournament_phase_recital
						has_current_phase = tournament_phase_ceremony
					}
				}
				activity_host = {
					OR = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_nomadic
						government_has_flag = government_is_herder
						government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_tournament_tribal.dds"

	}

			scope:activity = {

					limit = { exists = scope:contest_complete }
					scope:contest_complete = flag:recital
				}
				trigger_else = {
					OR = {
						has_current_phase = tournament_phase_recital
						has_current_phase = tournament_phase_ceremony
					}
				}
				activity_location ?= {
					OR = {
						culture ?= { has_graphical_mediterranean_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						steppe_building_gfx_use_mediterranean_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep3_feast_byzantine.dds"
		environment = "environment_ep3_byzantine_feast"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/corner_of_tavern"

ep2_wedding_ceremony = {
	background = {	 #Indian
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:activity }
				scope:activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_wedding }
			}
			OR = {
				location.culture ?= { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
				location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_wedding_ceremony_indian.dds"
		environment = "environment_indian_wedding"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Grand_Activities/Weddings/ep2_event_grand_wedding"
	}
	background = {	 #East Asian
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:activity }
				scope:activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_wedding }
			}
			location ?= {
				OR = {
					culture ?= { has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_wedding_ceremony_asia.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_wedding_ceremony_asia"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Grand_Activities/Weddings/ep2_event_grand_wedding"
	}
	background = {	 #MENA (also steppes and African )
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:activity }
				scope:activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_wedding }
			}
			OR = {
				location.culture ?= { has_graphical_mena_culture_group_trigger = yes }
				location.culture ?= { has_graphical_steppe_culture_group_trigger = yes }
				location.culture ?= { has_graphical_african_culture_group_trigger = yes }
				location.culture ?= { has_building_gfx = iranian_building_gfx }
				location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_wedding_ceremony_mena.dds"
		environment = "environment_mena_wedding"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Grand_Activities/Weddings/ep2_event_grand_wedding"

ep2_involved_activity = {
	### TOURNAMENT
	background = {
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {

				scope:bg_override_char = {
					involved_activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_tournament }
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				involved_activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_tournament }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_village_festival_western.dds"
		environment = "environment_village_festival"

	}
	### TOUR
	background = {	#Japanese
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }

					involved_activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_tour }
					location ?= {
						OR = {
							culture = { has_graphical_japanese_culture_group_trigger = yes }
							steppe_building_gfx_use_japanese_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				involved_activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_tour }
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						culture = { has_graphical_japanese_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						steppe_building_gfx_use_japanese_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		environment = "environment_tgp_tanabata_festival_night_japan"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_festival_generic_japan"

			trigger_if = {

					location ?= {

			}

				OR = {
					involved_activity.activity_location.culture = { has_building_gfx = arabic_group_building_gfx }

				scope:activity.activity_location.culture = { has_building_gfx = iranian_building_gfx }
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_feast_mena.dds"
		environment = "environment_mena_feast"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/evn_background_feast_mena"
	}
	background = { #Steppe
		trigger = {
			scope:activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_feast }
			scope:activity.activity_location.culture = { has_building_gfx = steppe_building_gfx }
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep2_feast_steppe.dds"

		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP2/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/evn_background_steppe"
	}
	background = { #East Asia
		trigger = {
			scope:activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_feast }
			scope:activity.location ?= {
				OR = {
					culture = { has_graphical_east_asia_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
				}
				}
			}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_feast_asia.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_feast_asia"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_feast_asia"
			}
	background = { #Feast Fallback
		trigger = {
			scope:activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_feast }
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/feast.dds"
		environment = "environment_event_feast"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/feasthall"
	}

	background = {	# EP3

			involved_activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_chariot_race }

	}

bp2_university = {
	background = { # Byzantium/Greek Everyone else
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location.culture ?= {
						# OR = {
							# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_byzantine
							# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_caucasian
						# }
						lotr_has_numenorean_culture_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location.culture ?= {
					# OR = {
						# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_byzantine
						# has_cultural_pillar = heritage_caucasian
					# }
					lotr_has_numenorean_culture_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/ep3_medi_study.dds"
		environment = "environment_ep3_byzantine_study"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/office_workplace"
	}
	background = {	#East Asia - uses the examination picture
		trigger = {
			location ?= {
				OR = {
					culture = { has_graphical_east_asia_or_southeast_asia_group_trigger = yes }
					steppe_building_gfx_use_east_asian_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/tgp_examination_room.dds"
		environment = "environment_tgp_examination_room"
		ambience = "event:/DLC/EP4/SFX/Events/Event_Backgrounds/tgp_examination_room"
	}
	background = {	#Western-ish University
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
					location.culture = {
						OR = {
							has_graphical_western_culture_group_trigger = yes
							has_graphical_norse_culture_group_trigger = yes
							has_graphical_iberian_culture_group_trigger = yes
							has_graphical_mediterranean_culture_group_trigger = yes
							}
						}
						location ?= {
							steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = no
							steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = no
							culture = { has_building_gfx = steppe_building_gfx }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
				location.culture = {
					OR = {
						has_graphical_western_culture_group_trigger = yes
						has_graphical_norse_culture_group_trigger = yes
						has_graphical_iberian_culture_group_trigger = yes
						has_graphical_mediterranean_culture_group_trigger = yes
						}
					}
					location ?= {
						steppe_building_gfx_use_mena_trigger = no
						steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = no
						culture = { has_building_gfx = steppe_building_gfx }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp2_university.dds"
		environment = "environment_bp2_university"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/BP2/bp2_university"
	}
	background = {	#Indian garden
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					OR = {
					location.culture = { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
						location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				OR = {
				location.culture = { has_graphical_india_culture_group_trigger = yes }
					location ?= { steppe_building_gfx_use_indian_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp2_indian_garden.dds"
		environment = "environment_bp2_garden_india_day"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/castle_garden_day"
	}
	background = {	#Fallback: Madrasa
		reference = "gfx/interface/illustrations/event_scenes/bp2_university_mena.dds"
		environment = "environment_bp2_university_mena"
		ambience = "event:/SFX/Events/Backgrounds/meetingchamber_western"
	}
}

terrain_settlement = {
	background = { # Hobbit Farmland, settled
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:bg_override_char }
				scope:bg_override_char = {
					location ?= {
						OR = {
							terrain = farmlands
							terrain = hills
							terrain = plains
						}
						exists = province_owner
						culture ?= { is_hobbit_culture = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				location ?= {
					OR = {
						terrain = farmlands
						terrain = hills
						terrain = plains

	}

						NOT = { is_dwarf = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {

					NOT = { is_dwarf = yes }
				}
			}
